具体根因: Network - POS Connection Issue

问题描述: Type:
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​
Double Precom for October 31 2025 POS capture

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:DOUBLE PRECOM
Root Cause Analysis: POS Offline

Resolution:
- Acknowledged the ticket.
- Coordinate with out R&D.
-Upon calling the store, when the cashier performed the pre-commit transaction, just before it was about to finish the POS suddenly went offline and a pop-up appeared which the cashier clicked "Confirm".-Additionally, cashier mentioned that there are duplicate pre-commit in E Treasury.
-According to our R&D.cloud shift handover timed out, and then offline shift handover was carried out. This resulted in two pieces of data in the cloud.
-Note:
The issue occurred due to unstable POS network connectivity at that time. The cloud successfully received the shift handover data once; however, the POS did not. Subsequently, the POS executed a local offline shift handover and re-uploaded the shift handover data.-Solution:
Temporary Solution:Manual data correction re-executing the generation of the E TREASURY file.
Long term Solution:Still under evaluation / Still considering a solution.
-Our R&D already done with the fix of SSM Marilao POS#031(TD 31/10/2025)
-The ticket is resolved.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​

SVI CEBU 0033-Upon checking with EOD failed .
-0 zero Amount of ISP
-NO EOD files created

Action Taken : Perform manual reconciliation

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI Cebu Reclamation TD: 11/02/2025

Root Cause Analysis:POS045 has an order (Receipt No.557436045251102194923090504​) that remained in a pending payment state due to the presence of two payment records (GCash INT and Other Tender) associated with it.Due tounstable network connectionduring the GCash payment process, the payment status query reached the Cloud Server first before the payment initiation.
Cashier used "Other Tender" to finish the transaction instead of using "Mark Success"

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda that this is the same issue previously encountered in SSM Pasig (Ticket No. 6027313, recorded in Problem 187).
3. Asked approval to fix the affected transaction.
4. R&D markedthe "GCash INT" payment status to "Payment Failed" in the Cloud database and reran the EOD files.
5.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

【POS PROBLEM】
问题: POS PROBLEM

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Briefly describe the issue/concerns and attach a screenshot or evidence:
CASHIERS UNABLE TO LOG-OUT DUE TO POS OFFLINE, HOWEVER WE CHECKED ON DMALL SYSTEM THE TRANSACTION OF POS 5 AND POS 6 ARE INDICATE ON SYSTEM, EXCEPT THE POS 8 THE TRA

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:User Knowledge


Issue Description:POS PROBLEM​

Troubleshooting process:

Good day! This is a known scenario. Based on the findings from our R&D Team, this behavior occurs when the POS terminal is offline (either no network or the POS can't connect to ISP and Cloud) and there are still pending transactions that have not yet been uploaded.
When the cashier attempts to perform a pre-commit while the system is in this state, a prompt message will appear:
POS is offline. Confirm log out?
Offline transactions have not been uploaded completely and EOD might be affected if log out. Confirm proceeding?”


This message serves as a warning that not all offline transactions have been synchronized with cloud and ISP. Proceeding with the pre-commit could result in incomplete data being reflected in the End of Day (EOD) reports.
If the cashier clicks Confirm, the system will proceed to generate a Pre-Commit and Cashier X Reading Receipts, and  will automatically logged out after the pre-commit process. However, since the transactions have not been fully uploaded, this may affect the accuracy of the EOD report or cause discrepancies in sales data once the POS reconnects online.
If the cashier clicks Cancel instead, this action will stop the pre-commit process: no Pre-Commit and Cashier X Reading Receipts will be generated, and the cashier will remain logged in until the POS goes back online and all pending transactions are successfully uploaded.

However, if the cashier does not click either Cancel or Confirm, the POS will automatically lock due to inactivity after several seconds.
 As a result, it will also affect Terminal-Z.

【DMallAppsConcerns - SVI Fairview 0019 October 30, 2025 Incorrect SI POS061 Online POS】
问题: DMallAppsConcerns - SVI Fairview 0019 October 30, 2025 Incorrect SI POS061 Online POS

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Configuration / Setup Issue

问题描述: Good day!







We would like to inform you that our R&D Team found that on SVI Fairview, POS061 Online POS has incorrect SI on October 30, 2025.







Store Name:SVI FAIRVIEW 0019


Receipt No: 555191061251030164646150040


SI

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
1.The cashier tried torecall an orderwhile theinternet was slow or lagging.2.Because there wasno loading screen on the POS, the cashier thought nothing happened, so she also clicked“Online Sales.”at the same time.
3.While the system was lagging, theold suspended orderwas still in thetemporary database.
4.After restarting the POS, that suspended orderappeared again, but the data gotmixed up— causing aduplicate SI (Sales Invoice)number.

How to reproduce the issue:
1.There’s asuspended orderin POS.
2.But network must be poor.
3.When you click“Recall Order”(only one recall order) and thenetwork is poor, there’sno response. Then youquickly click the “Online Sales”button.









4.At the same time, thenetwork recovers, and thensome online receipts are printed.






5.multiple SIs (8, 9, 10, 11)are printed.



6.Thenclose the online order page.
​




7.Butthere are no items.





8. Thenrestart the POS, but after restarting, thecart is not empty.




9.Thensubmit this order.




10.SI got duplicated.




Long Term - Solution:
-When clicking the“Recall Order”button, add aloading pageso that the“Online Sales”button cannot be clicked.





our R&D Team has resolved the issue withOrder #555191061251030164646150040.
TheSI numberhas been corrected to0000008034, and allSI numbers are now properly sequenced.

Material
Material Description
QTY

0507

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
 The store overscanned the affected articles, which resulted in over-serving. They confirmed that the actual items received versus the plan quantity are aligned. 【POS 38 CANNOT PROCEED TO TRANSACTION】
问题: POS 38 CANNOT PROCEED TO TRANSACTION

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Hardware - POS Restart / Shutdown

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:​
CANNOT PROCEED TRANSACTION DUE TO SI#CONTINUITY EXCEPTION, PLEASE CONTACT IT FOR HELP.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:Cashier Force Shutdown the POS038


Issue Description:POS 38 CANNOT PROCEED TO TRANSACTION​

Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the Ticket.
2. Report in our R&D Team.
3.The POS38 encountered the SI#Continuity error.
.
4. Based on the conversation with the store:
- According to the store personnel, when cashierMa. Johanna Clarisse Abajawas performing the pre-commit, she was unable to enter any numbers in the POS because a Windows message appeared promptingCtrl + Alt + Delete. As a result, the cashier was forced to shut down the POS, which subsequently caused database corruption.

5. Findings of R&D Team:
-Based on the log, the POS was restarted after 20:12. However, by that time, the database had already been corrupted. All data from November 6 in the POS local database is missing, resulting in a discontinuity of the SI sequence.


  



6. Root Cause:
Due to a forced shutdown, the database was corrupted, and even the backup database cannot be restored. Our R&D Team still considering other possible solutions.
7. Temporary Solution:
- Manually construct the Terminal- Z for dated November 6, 2025.

8. Maam Chanda approved the Fix Data.
9.our R&D Team has completed the fix data forPOS038. nd theSI numbersare properly sequenced.
10. Resolved.

【Cashiers with large amount of  shortages, un tally counts of SD and more than 4 times pick up. Also we notice that the business date at IN STORE RECONCILLATION MGT is still Nov. 5, 2025】
问题: Cashiers with large amount of  shortages, un tally counts of SD and more than 4 times pick up. Also we notice that the business date at IN STORE RECONCILLATION MGT is still Nov. 5, 2025

根因分类: Network / Connectivity Failure

具体根因: Network - ISP Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​

Cashiers with large amount of shortages, un tally counts of SD and more than 4 times pick up. Also we notice that the business date at IN STORE RECONCILLATION

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS pre-commit and pickup data are not accurate

Root Cause Analysis:POS connection issue
POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud during shift handover; uses the POS local data.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with DMall R&D.
2.Based on the logs and continuous ping, the POScan't connect to the ISP and the Cloud during shift handover therefore the system utilized the POS local data for the pre-commit and pickup records.
3. Also based on the monitoring tool, the ISP of SSM Molino was offline for over two days, from 11/3/2025 15:46:10 to 11/5/2025 23:33:12. 
4. Informed the store that the pre-commit data may not be fully accurate; however, the POS Real-time Sales and Term-Z net amounts remain balanced. Therefore, no discrepancies are expected during the Accounting audit. This behavior is considered normal under such circumstances.
5. Resolved the ticket.

Response Level:Level A / B / C / D

Good day.

We are experiencing long lagging posting of GRS for more than one hour. 
We have good network connection. 
Ramdom PO's are affected on lagging posting of

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:SLOW PROCESS IN POSTING 

Root Cause Analysis: DMall Defect

Resolution:

- The store is processing their receiving, however the print of GRS is slow.
- Upon checking this is a system bug. Due to the duplicate data it causes the system to be busy and make the status of the P.O still Posting.
- Temporary Solution: DMall R&D change the batch query configuration and restart the server after getting approval to Ms. Cathy Canlas.
- Long-term solution: Add to Problem No. 264 to fix the bug.
- Store confirmed that they are able to see now the GR number.
- No further assistance needed.
- Closing as resolved.

解决方案:
Define Issue:SLOW PROCESS IN POSTING 

Root Cause Analysis: DMall Defect

Resolution:

- The store is processing their receiving, however the print of GRS is slow.
- Upon checking this is a system bug. Due to the duplicate data it causes the system to be busy and make the status of the P.O still Posting.
- Temporary Solution: DMall R&D change the batch query configuration and restart the server after getting approval to Ms. Cathy Canlas.
- Long-term solution: Add to Problem No. 264 to fix the bug.
- Store confirmed that they are able to see now the GR number.
- No further assistance needed.
- Closing as resolved.

根因分类: SAP Std Functionality

具体根因: Software - Document Locking

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template






Contact Person: *




DMall Support Team






Contact Number / MS Teams: *




09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:SVI MANILA [0092] Integration Inventory 2025 November 7 - Error Msg: User NHOSCHSU06 already processing Purchasing document 2035223158 and 2035250196

Root Cause Analysis:Document Locking

Resolution:
Created a ticket for integration error.
Based on historical/previous tickets, the error occurred becauseuser "NHOSCHSU06" is currently accessing the document while it's being posted in DMall. This is standard behavior in SAP; if a document or article is being used by another user, it won't allow simultaneous posting.
Advised the store to repost the order number to generate new GR in SAP.
Store reposted the order number and has now a GR.
Will now proceed in resolving this ticket.

Remarks/Recommendation: -

- Temporary Solution: DMall R&D change the batch query configuration and restart the server after getting approval to Ms. Cathy Canlas.
- Long-term solution: Add to Problem No. 264 to fix the bug.
- Store confirmed that they are able to see now the GR number.
- No further assistance needed.
- Closing as resolved.

【not aligned inventory in SAP versus Dmall of article no.20185557】
问题: not aligned inventory in SAP versus Dmall of article no.20185557

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​


Dear Ma'am/Sir,
Asking for your assistance pls. This is with regards to ff.item wherein,
Dmall inventory is negative (-)2 while SAP is already zero(0) invent

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Based on further checking in SAP, the 971 and 972 movements are the offsetting jobs for consignment without inventory. Since the corresponding movement is not present in our DMall system, this has caused the discrepancy, particularly the reversal (972 movement) in SAP, which was not reflected in DMall.
To resolve this promptly, OPC should clean up the inventory of the article in the DMall system.

【CASHIER ENCOUNTER SHORTAGES】
问题: CASHIER ENCOUNTER SHORTAGES

根因分类: Network / Connectivity Failure

具体根因: Network - POS Connection Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level D
Details of Issue:
please be inform that 4 of our cashiers today encounter shortages thru double pick up and no of sales draft become twice. instead 8 sales draft it became 16.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS pre-commit and pickup data are not accurate

Root Cause Analysis:POS connection issue
POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud during shift handover; uses the POS local data.

Resolution:
Regarding the pre-commit and pickup records, please note that the system utilized the POS local data during the shift handover for the POS that cashier's used, as these terminals can't connect to the ISP and the Cloud at that time(Figure 2).
Additionally, based on our Monitoring tool, the ISP of SSM Sucat was offline for over two days, from2025-11-04 09:31:03to2025-11-06 23:37:32(Figure 1).
You may check the attached screenshots for reference.As a result, the pre-commit data may not be fully accurate; however, the POS Real-time Sales and Term-Z net amounts remain balanced. Therefore, no discrepancies are expected during the Accounting audit.
For your information, this behavior is considered normal under such circumstances.
Thank you for your understanding.
Figure 1. POS and ISP Offline Monitoring Tool



Figure 2. POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud logs
​

解决方案:
Define Issue: SSM FORTUNE KING SABANG NAIC [6835] Integration Inventory 2025 November 07 - Error Msg: User WHS5RSOF1 already processing Purchasing document 2035133305
Root Cause Analysis: Integration Failure
Resolution:
Create an integration ticket.Advice the store to repost this order number using the manager's account.
Upon reposting, there was a pop up message showed " There is no re - post item"


Investigation:
As per our R&D, theDelivery Notes0074434930,0074395811, and0074415085were received underID16835202511080001, and this receiving record was successfully synchronized to SAP.
However, since these DNs belong to two different orders, the SAP document number was incorrectly updated to the receiving recordID16835202511050001instead.

Proposed Solution:
SM will need to perform an inventory adjustment for DN0074434930,0074395811, and0074415085using movement type170/171, as these DNs were received twice on the Dmall side.
ForID16835202511050001, our R&D team will manually tag the corresponding DN items as“No Need.”
Meanwhile, forID16835202511080001, R&D will manually update the SAP document number to the correct receiving record.
Proceed on resolving.

【NO TERM Z ALL POS NOV.11 2025】
问题: NO TERM Z ALL POS NOV.11 2025

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
No TERMZ ALL POS Nov.11,2025

Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
​
Details of Issue: I check the dmall dashboard for the TERMZ receipt but no records

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: User Knowledge- inform the store about the how system was design for generation of terminal - Z


Issue Description:NO TERM Z ALL POS NOV.11 2025​


Troubleshooting process:


Please be informed that the Terminal-Z report is automatically generated by the system at the end of each day, specifically at11:59 PM.

This is part of the system’s built-in design.

Although it’s possible to manually generate a Terminal-Z report using the “Manual Terminal-Z” button, we do not recommend doing so since the store usually has many customers. For this reason, the system is configured to automatically generate the Terminal-Z report before the day ends (11:59 PM).

【OVER GR PROCESSED IN DELIVERY】
问题: OVER GR PROCESSED IN DELIVERY

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:​


Good day Mam / Sir

Fyi po, we have encountered over GR of P.O # 1106449588 with GR # 5111622858 under vendor Maryland distributors inc that subject for reversal.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
The root cause of this ticket is that the SMCo trainer mistakenly reversed the GR directly in SAP instead of in Dmall. When the ERS was created, the GR had already been reversed, resulting in a zero amount, which made the ERS non-reversible.

OPC reversed the PO in Dmall, however the reversal was failed due to ERS non-reversable that's why Dmall tagged the reference order to No Need.

result/behavior)NO CAPTURED EJ ON DMALL OS FOR POS 1 AND 8 ON NOV EMB

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:User Knowledge- inform the store for the logic of the system.


Issue Description:RE:DECAMALL NO CAPTURED EJ ON DMALL OS FOR POS 1 AND 8 ON NOV.11,2025


Troubleshooting process:
upon checking, the terminal - Z are all generated the next day after the cashier sign-on.

please refer to the image below.
POS001



POS008


The terminal - Z are automatically generated before the end of day specifically 11:59PM. but if the cashier forgets to log out, it will generate the next day after cashier sign-out. Other scenerio is, if the DMall application is exited/not open, the terminal - Z will generate the next day after cashier sign-on.

【Unaligned inventory vs SAP】
问题: Unaligned inventory vs SAP

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:​

We have an archived article that does not match on DMALL vs SAP. Article should be zero on our system inventory, since we already requested to OPC for the settlement of the article

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue:
 A movement type 311 transaction posted in SAP on 10/22/2025 (material document 4909029665, processed by user NHOOPCVP01) recorded -2 PC in Sloc 1 and +2 PC in Sloc 3. However, this transaction is not reflected in the DMall system, causing a discrepancy in inventory:
SAP inventory: Sloc 1 = 0 PC, Sloc 3 = 0 PC
DMall inventory: Sloc 1 = -2 PC, Sloc 3 = +2 PC
All other movements are consistent between SAP and DMall, with a total quantity adjustment of -64 PC.
Resolution:
 OPC should apply the same adjustment in DMall for Sloc 1 and Sloc 3 as recorded in SAP to ensure both systems reflect the correct inventory.

【SMCo HEADOFFICE [8880] Integration Purchase 2025 November 12 - Error Msg: 10 : Receive Inventory Location are not available】
问题: SMCo HEADOFFICE [8880] Integration Purchase 2025 November 12 - Error Msg: 10 : Receive Inventory Location are not available

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template






Contact Person: *




DMall Support Team






Contact Number / MS Teams: *




09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:SMCo HEADOFFICE [8880] Integration Purchase 2025 November 12 - Error Msg: 10 : Receive Inventory Location are not availableRoot Cause Analysis:Integration Failure

Resolution:
We found an integration ticket and made a ticket for it.
We coordinated the issue to our R&D and found out that the configured Storage location for the POs is 0031 whilst 0031 is notincluded in the receiving inventory storage location of the store.
We then coordinated this to Functional team and asked Master Data team to add SLoc 0031 to site 8880.
After adding it, Functional Team clicked the repair button and all POs can now be viewable in Order query.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.

【RESTRICTION OF SM BONUS WHOLE CHICKEN ARTICLES 10S】
问题: RESTRICTION OF SM BONUS WHOLE CHICKEN ARTICLES 10S

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Request
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue: 11-13-2025

We would like to request restriction for the articles listed below to all SVI Sites. These items remain readable on the Weighing Scales and DMALL as of Nov 3.&

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:​User Knowledge -inform the requester regarding the DMall system logic, allows any article with a defined price to be scanned on POS or weighed at Weighing Scale.​

Issue Description:RESTRICTION OF SM BONUS WHOLE CHICKEN ARTICLES 10S​


Troubleshooting process:




Upon checking inDMall OS (Store Article Management), we found that articles20497631and20497632are tagged as“No”in theSellablecolumn. This is the reason why the POS displays the message“Article is Restricted.”


However, these articles remainweighableon the weighing scale because, in bothStore Article ManagementandScale Article Management, they still have aGross Selling Price of ₱1.00. The DMall system logic allows any article with a defined price to be scanned on POS or weighed at Weighing Scale.






Therefore, if you wish torestrictthese articles from being weighed on the scale, according to our R&D Team, you mayset their Gross Selling Price to ₱0.00, which will prevent them from being processed on the weighing scale.

【POS is offline upon Pre commit of the Cashier (All POS)】
问题: POS is offline upon Pre commit of the Cashier (All POS)

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: POS is offline. Confrm log out?
 Offline transactios have not been uploaded completely and EOD might be affected if log out. Confirm proceeding?

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:"POS is offline. Confirm logout?" message prompt in POS

Root Cause Analysis:User Knowledge
When the POS can't connect to the ISP or Cloud and there are pending or unuploaded sales/EJ, the cashier must click“Confirm”to log out (see Figure 1 below).

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2. Informed the requester about the behavior of POS if itcan't connect to ISP/Cloud and there are pending or unuploaded sales/EJ to the Cloud and ISP.
3.Advised the store to check the POS connectivity status before performing the Pre-Commit, or click“Confirm”when the prompt message appears on the POS screen to prevent this issue from recurring.Resolved the ticket.

SSM ETON (0757)

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SSM Eton TD: 11/13/2025

Root Cause Analysis:SSM Eton POS007 has an order(Receipt No.559246007251113145306750104)that remained in a pending payment state due to the presence of two payment records associated with it (QRPH).
Due tounstable network connectionduring the payment process, the payment status query reached the Cloud Server first before the payment initiation.

3. Asked approval to fix the affected transaction.

【POS problem lane 5】
问题: POS problem lane 5

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Hardware - POS Restart / Shutdown

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: Nov 15,2025 at 8:42PM

POS promting SI# continuity exception,
POS ID : 28001
MAC : 68-ED-A4-89-3B-84

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:User Error Cashier's Force shutdown the POS005

​
Issue Description:POS problem lane 5​

Troubleshooting process:
Conversation with Store Supervisor:
-Upon calling the store, the cashier stated that after waiting for the receipt to print, the POS experienced hanging and continuous loading. She added that she forcefully clicked the button to restart the POS. After the forced restart, an SI Continuity Exception appeared on the POS. The cashier forcefully restarted the pos several times.
-Additionally, it is the 1st time that this POS hangs. 



Investigation of R&D Team:
1.Based on the logs, when the order #557711005251115204218230158was completed at2025-11-15 20:42:24.035, the POS hardware restarted on2025-11-15 20:42:34.158and goes up at2025-11-15 20:42:40.358. It is for about 6seconds.
2.And at2025-11-15 20:36:33.256, it is the time when POS application was launched again.




3.We checked the Continuous PIng for this POS unfortunately, there is no Continuous Ping for November 15, 2025.
4.Additionally, this POS did not encounter Windows Update.
Impact:
1.Due on this abnormal POS hardware restart, the POS Local Database did not increase which caused the SI# Continuity message on the POS.


Temporary Solution:
-Our R&D Team will modify the sequence in POS Local Database. The sequence record was 21737 which needs to be increased to 21738 so that when the POS used again, the next order SI should be 21738.




for reference:The SI exception serves as a built-in safeguard in the POS system to prevent sequence discontinuity of SI numbers. When a discontinuity is detected, the POS is intentionally disabled to ensure data integrity. Our R&D Team will continue to optimize the mechanism for handling SI exceptions to minimize future occurrences.
Long Term Solution:
-It is recorded in problem Management No# 143(POS suddenly crash caused inconsecutive SI) and will be included in the November Special Release.

Maam Chanda approved with the Fix and our R&D Team done fixing the data of POS005.
Resolved.

【dc crossdock/bst delivery】
问题: dc crossdock/bst delivery

根因分类: Others

具体根因: Apps - Data Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A /
Details of Issue:​

dc crossdock/bst delivery last nov 05, 2025 not yet posted still posting in status no GRS generated

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause Analysis:Upon checking seal no. 2664555-60, it turns out that the DN under that seal was already GI’d and released in DMall on different dates, which overwrote the first DNs that were released. As for seal no. 3402609-14, several DNs under that seal were changed to a new seal by the DC on November 17, 2025.


Resolution:1. Dmall will manually mark the DNs that are tagged “No” under Data Available column in Dmall to “Yes” and move it to a new purchase order of seal no.2664555-60 & 3402609-14.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - EOD Failure

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SVI EO (EAST ORTIGAS)
Sitecode: 1968-----------------------------------
Findings/Caused:
-Upon checking with successful End Of Day but still no EOD files creat

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI East Ortigas TD: 11/17/2025

Root Cause Analysis:POS014 has an order(Receipt No.557641014251117090541000021)that remained in a pending payment state due to absence of payment data(BDO Credit).
The payment record exists in the POS local database. However, there was a delay in writing the payment data, which caused it to be missing when the order was pushed to the Cloud.
According to R&D, such delays can occur for several reasons, including concurrent data writes or access by other software (e.g., antivirus programs).

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda about the findings and temporary solution.
3. Asked approval to fix the affected transaction.
4. R&D updated the data and add the missing payment record for the affected orderand reran the EOD files.
5.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

解决方案:
Define Issue:SSM NORTH EDSA [0269] Integration Inventory 2025 November 18 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 1 PC : 20154393 0269 0003
Root Cause Analysis: Timing Issue

Resolution:
-The problem of the sequence of two pieces of documentation has led to a push failure IO10269202511180019, IO10269202511180021.
- IO10269202511180019 should be pushed first, followed by IO10269202511180021. Both transaction request are on the millisecond level. 
- Informed IT Team and they confirmed DMall can manually repost the transaction since it is only a timing issue. 
- Reposted the transaction and it was successful with SAP No. 4909835471.
- No further asisstance needed. Closing as resolved.

【DMallAppsConcern - SSM 589524 2025 November 18 Missing Barcode Information】
问题: DMallAppsConcern - SSM 589524 2025 November 18 Missing Barcode Information

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Dear Maam Chanda,







We would like to inform you that our R&D Team an alert On SSM Tenant (589524) and found that several orders were missing item barcodes in the order details, which caused the sales transaction records to fail generati

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:Defect from DMall


Issue Description:DMallAppsConcern - SSM 589524 2025 November 18 Missing Barcode Information

Troubleshooting process:
our R&D Team received an alert for Tenant (589524) covering stores SSM Novaliches (0763), SSM Rosales (0753), SSM Congressional (1758), and SSM Daet (1200). The investigation showed that certain orders from these stores had missing item barcodes in their order details, resulting in failed generation of sales transaction records. Since these orders are already closed, this issue will cause tonight’s EOD upload to fail.

Orders that were affected:

      Store                  Receipt#                       Article Code          Barcode
1.SSM Novaliches 0763      559251026251118135125480067                 20192385                        2876400000000           
                       559251007251118134759100049               2009913                        2850332000000

2.SSM Rosales (0753)          559326035251118141438710004     20031050                           2861959000000
3.SSM Congressional (1758)     559216017251118133725930040              20031046                           2861955000000
4.SSM Daet (1200)             559446010251118141547460022               10054850007                        2856167000000


Investigation:
Our R&D findings show that during order processing, some items within the affected orders were being manually updated by Masterdata at the same time. As a result, when the system queried the item information, the barcode data was missing.

Solution:
-Our R&D Team will manually add/restore the missing item barcodes to the order information.

Maam Chanda Approved and Our R&D Team proceed with the fix data and added in problem 273for internal discussion of long-term solution on how to handle these kinds of scenerios if will happen again in the future.

Resolved.​
